<span>4 to 6 sprigs fresh basil , plus 2 tablespoons finely shredded leaves for garnish</span> 
<span>3. Remove chicken from oven and turn oven temperature to 475 degrees ( use convection feature if you have it ) . Or , preheat broiler and arrange oven rack about 8 inches from the heat. </span> 
<span>4. Return uncovered pan to oven and cook until chicken skin is browned , cooking liquid is reduced , and vegetables are very soft , 10 to 15 minutes more. </span> 
<span>5. Remove and discard basil sprigs. Garnish with shredded basil and serve immediately.</span>

Instead of pasta , use 1/2 pound moderately starchy potatoes like Yukon Golds or fingerlings. Slice or dice and add to water at the beginning of Step 1. Simmer until tender , 10 to 15 minutes. 
Substitute 1/3 cup rice or quinoa for pasta. Add in Step 1 and simmer until cooked , 10 to 15 minutes. 
Substitute 1 cup cooked brown rice , farro or other whole grains for pasta. Cook separately; warm and spoon into bowls before spooning soup on top. 
Instead of beating 2 eggs and stirring in , poach 4 eggs right in the soup or separately , and place one in each bowl.
